        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[AttachmentId] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C1]
        FROM   (SELECT TOP (2) 
            [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
            [Extent1].[CommunityId] AS [CommunityId],

            WHERE ([Extent1].[IsDeleted] <> 1) AND ([Extent1].[Id] = @p__linq__0) ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[AttachmentId] AS [AttachmentId], [Extent2].[HouseId] AS [HouseId], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name], [Extent3].[IconName] AS [IconName], [Extent3].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], [Extent3].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted]

    )  AS [Project2]
    ORDER BY [Project2].[Id] ASC, [Project2].[C1] ASC
